A fierce battle is expected near Maoer Mountain. (16th dispatch)

(Harbin) This morning, the Mifeng Station near Maoer Mountain Station was attacked by bandits. The railway cargo depot and the residences of railway staff were robbed. The railway staff, lacking protection, have fled elsewhere. Yesterday, five freight cars were derailed near Shitouhezi and attacked by bandits. When the repair crew arrived, they were also attacked. (15th Reuters dispatch)

(Harbin) The situation in northern Manchuria is becoming increasingly complex. The Self-Defense Army, not the Manchurian state army, is definitely in control of the overall situation. Government troops stationed in various small towns have joined the Self-Defense Army one after another, and in several places, upon hearing that the Self-Defense Army is about to attack, they flee and surrender to the other side. The Manchurian state army has now acquired a new name, "Baomingjun" (Life-Preserving Army), meaning that they can do everything but fight for the (new) country. After Ma Zhanshan's defection, the momentum of the Self-Defense Army greatly increased. Ma recently went to Qiqihar to pack up his furniture and dismiss his servants. Japanese Army Attempts to Inspect Soviet Consulate in Harbin 80

Harbin Police Chief Refuses

(Moscow) A telegram has been received here from Blagoveshchensk, reporting that the Japanese army in Harbin is actively attempting to provoke a serious dispute between the Soviet Union and the Manchurian government. It is said that these Japanese troops are firmly demanding that the Chinese authorities in Harbin inspect the Soviet consulate in that city. The reason for the demand for inspection is the false accusation that the Soviet Consul General is planning terrorist acts to sabotage the Chinese Eastern Railway. Although it is clear that the bridge bombing incident was orchestrated by White Russians, a reliable source reports that the Japanese military in Harbin held a meeting on the 12th of this month and decided to demand that the Chinese police in that city carry out this plan to inspect the Soviet consulate. The mastermind behind this is a Japanese advisor to the Harbin Chinese Police Department. However, despite the urging of the Japanese advisor, the head of the Harbin Police Department, Wang Qihua, refused, saying that he had not received direct orders from the Manchurian government in Changchun. The real reason for his refusal is that the Japanese advisor insisted that the action appear to be carried out independently and voluntarily by the Chinese police. It is said that when the Japanese advisor asked Chief Wang to carry out the inspection, he stated that this matter must absolutely not be known to the outside world as being directed by the Japanese army. (15th TASS dispatch)

Soviet Communiqué Comments on Japanese Provocative Behavior 81

Containing a Special Political Effect

(Moscow) The Soviet government's newspaper, Izvestia, today published a long editorial entitled "Continuous New Provocations in Manchuria." It stated that recent incidents in the area under the jurisdiction of the new government in Manchuria are quite noteworthy and suspicious. Suspected Russian conspiracy cases have been discovered one after another, and they seem to be directly linked to the actions of the Manchurian police and to the counter-propaganda of Japanese and White Russian newspapers. The provocative act of bombing the Songhua River Bridge occurred just as the famous White Russian leader Semenov was openly negotiating with powerful figures in Tokyo. After this negotiation, Japanese and Manchurian newspapers uniformly began a new attack on the Soviet Union. The methods of the Japanese newspapers are quite bizarre. They want to link the White Russian bridge bombing case on the Songhua River with the Harbin military vehicle accident and the unfounded rumors that Ma Zhanshan fled to Hailanpao, using them as an excuse to demand that the Japanese authorities in Manchuria take resolute action against a certain country. Japanese journalists shamelessly imitate the tone of politicians, vaguely saying that a certain country has recently planned to launch red terrorist sabotage activities. (The country they are referring to is obviously the Soviet Union). It is clear that their intention is to provoke a dispute between Japan and the Soviet Union. The Japanese newspaper in Harbin even stated that the Eastern Branch of the Communist International is related to Zhang Xueliang and the Kuomintang. The only deficiency is that the newspaper did not say that Gandhi and Hitler were both involved in the conspiracy to bomb the Songhua River Bridge. In short, those who can see clearly can understand this reversal of right and wrong. Their true intentions are even more evident in the recent rumors about Ma Zhanshan. We all know that at the beginning of the Manchurian Incident, the Japanese falsely accused General Ma of having relations with the Soviet Union and of receiving Soviet aid. Then a document was discovered, revealing that the Japanese themselves were transporting military supplies to General Ma. After that, General Ma settled matters peacefully with the Japanese and became an important official in the new Manchurian state. Now, the Japanese are again claiming that he has a relationship with the Soviet Union. However, today's statement issued by TASS has fundamentally refuted this rumor. Ma's speculative actions this time were obviously directed by the Japanese in order for the Japanese to create rumors that he had a relationship with the Soviet Union. These rumors are just as unfounded as the earlier reports in Japanese newspapers about the relationship between Ding Chao, Li Du, and the Soviet Union, and about the Soviet Union sending terrorists to Harbin to destroy the White Russian registration office. According to Izvestia's speculation, this continuous provocative behavior contains a special political effect. It intends to show the state of unrest in Manchuria in order to create an excuse for increasing the Japanese army. Regarding this point, a Tokyo newspaper specially published a document from the French military, stating that the new government in Manchuria has shown itself to be unable to maintain order, and it is quite necessary for the Japanese army to increase its forces. Izvestia pointed out another reason for the Japanese newspapers' continuous provocation and rumor-mongering: the League of Nations Inquiry Commission is about to arrive in Manchuria. The Japanese warlords want to use this despicable method to show the guests from Geneva that the Japanese troops occupying Manchuria and the White Russian troops there are "guardians of civilization." Although those who plot provocation want to use the Manchurian incident to incite a war in the Far East, their goal may not be easily achieved. Since the incident occurred, the Soviet Union has consistently adhered to its policy of peace abroad and protection of the interests of all workers at home. The Soviet Union will expose these conspiracies as much as possible, but will not be provoked to escalate the situation. (15th TASS dispatch)

Luo Wengan's Desire to Resign 82

The Executive Yuan Urged Him to Stay and Returned His Resignation

Shen Jin Ding's Talk:

Regarding the South Manchurian Railway Parallel Line Issue

(Nanjing) Luo Wengan resigned from his positions as Minister of Justice and concurrently Minister of Foreign Affairs. The Executive Yuan urged him to stay. (Special dispatch, 15th)

(Nanjing) Luo resigned from all his concurrent posts. The State Council decided to return the original resignation. (Special dispatch, 16th)

(Nanjing) At 11 a.m. on the 16th, Shen Jin Ding, Director of the Asian Department of the Ministry of Foreign Affairs, received reporters from the capital on behalf of Minister Luo and made the following statement: Minister Luo is attending a meeting of the Executive Yuan and asked me to receive you on his behalf. Now, I will talk to you about the recent diplomatic situation. (1) Regarding the issue of parallel lines of the South Manchurian Railway, the Reuters report of Minister Luo's last conversation differed greatly from what Minister Luo actually said. Now, I will briefly explain to you. The so-called parallel lines are recorded in the minutes of the meeting supplementary to the Sino-Japanese Conference on Matters Concerning the Three Eastern Provinces in 1905. The Japanese version, which they call a secret agreement, differs slightly from the original text of the minutes. The original text states: "For the purpose of maintaining the interests of the Eastern Provinces Railway, the Chinese government agrees not to build parallel main lines or branch lines that would damage the interests of the railway near the railway before the recovery of the railway." This statement is recorded in the minutes and not included in the treaty. It is only kept in the minutes, so it has no effect as a treaty. Even the minutes themselves only have the signatures of the Chinese and Japanese representatives attending the meeting and do not have a seal, so they are certainly different from a treaty. For many years, what Japan has regarded as a parallel line and opposed has been the Datong Line. The Datong Line is more than 100 miles away from the South Manchurian Railway. It is not near it and its direction is not completely parallel. Even knowledgeable Japanese people, such as Professor Yokota of Tokyo Imperial University, have commented that the Datong Line cannot be considered a parallel line of the South Manchurian Railway. If the Datong Line is said to be parallel to the South Manchurian Railway, then the Tokaido Line and the Chuo Line on Honshu, Japan, can also be considered parallel. This shows that justice resides in people's hearts and legal principles cannot be ignored. Furthermore, statistics prove that the South Manchurian Railway's profits have not decreased due to the opening of the Datong Line. The recent decrease in the South Manchurian Railway's profits is due to its own management, which is too bureaucratic, and the impact of high gold prices. The Japanese side cannot subjectively blame the Datong Line, saying that it has damaged the interests of the South Manchurian Railway. In addition, the Xi'an Line is also considered by the Japanese side to be parallel to the South Manchurian Railway. This line is not only not parallel to the South Manchurian Railway, but is also further away, so it certainly cannot damage the interests of the railway. Moreover, China is using its own funds to build railways in its own territory to promote the economic development of the Northeast. Why should foreigners interfere? Furthermore, the Northeast has vast lands. In addition to the South Manchurian Railway, several more railways can be built. How can foreigners subjectively and arbitrarily oppose the construction of one or two more lines? (2) Regarding the Shanghai Ceasefire Conference, the Shanghai Ceasefire Conference was held based on a resolution of the League of Nations General Assembly. Now, the conference is stalled because Japan is exceeding the scope of the discussion of the ceasefire conference. Although the ceasefire conference is now deadlocked, the subcommittee meetings continue to be held, which proves that our side has no intention of breaking up the ceasefire conference. Unexpectedly, recently, the Japanese representatives in the subcommittee meetings have again raised issues outside the scope, which ultimately led to the adjournment of the subcommittee meetings. Our side certainly cannot bear any responsibility. Now, we are only waiting for a fair explanation from the League of Nations Special Committee. As for the policy to be adopted by our government, it is currently under careful consideration. According to today's news, it is said that the Japanese government seems to have instructed its representatives not to participate in the League of Nations Special Committee. If this is true, it is tantamount to saying that Japan does not want to be a member of the League of Nations and may place itself in an isolated position internationally. This kind of statement is the same as the argument that the country wants to withdraw from the League of Nations. Now, I will comment on the argument that Japan is withdrawing from the League of Nations. Recently, many Japanese have advocated withdrawing from the League of Nations. I personally feel that there are doubts as to whether these people have a deep understanding of the League of Nations Covenant. The Covenant stipulates that two years' notice must be given before withdrawing from the League of Nations, and all due responsibilities must be fulfilled one by one. Moreover, this matter has a significant relationship to Japan itself. After the European War, Japan was entrusted by the League of Nations to govern Yap Island. If it withdraws from the League of Nations, it must return the island to the League of Nations. Would Japan be willing to abandon it so hastily? Therefore, the argument of withdrawing from the League of Nations is probably just a high-sounding statement. (3) Regarding the issue of the pseudo-organization in the Northeast refusing to allow Gu's representatives to enter Manchuria, it is heard that the Japanese side has expressed informally that if the investigation team inspects the South Manchurian Railway line, it should bear the responsibility of protection. Where the investigation team intends to go should be decided by the team itself and not be subject to restrictions from any party. As the Northeast is a part of China's territory, our government will send appropriate troops to accompany them and be responsible for protecting the entire investigation team. This is currently under careful consideration. (Special dispatch, 16th)

Executive Yuan Discusses Countermeasures to the Diplomatic Situation 83

Guo Taiqi Reports on the Negotiations

It is Said That Concrete Measures Have Been Decided

Telegraph to Yan Huiqing to Instruct Him on Matters

(Nanjing) The Executive Yuan held meetings on both the morning and afternoon of the 16th, chaired by Wang Zhaoming, to discuss the issue of Sino-Japanese diplomacy. Guo Taiqi reported on the breakdown of the ceasefire conference and presented all his views. The discussion on future countermeasures was very detailed. However, due to strict confidentiality, the content of the meeting was not released. It is only heard that concrete measures have been decided. A telegram was immediately sent to Yan Huiqing to supplement his report to the League of Nations Special Committee and instruct him on matters. Countermeasures were also discussed regarding the issue of the pseudo-state refusing to allow Gu to accompany the investigation team out of the pass. The entire organization of the League of Nations investigation team cannot be slightly affected by the unreasonable opposition of the pseudo-state. The investigation team has made a strict statement. Our diplomatic authorities have protested against the Japanese initiative in this matter. The responsibility for future security issues will naturally be assigned. Moreover, because the Northeast is our country's territory, if necessary, we will use force to protect all members of the team out of the pass. (Special dispatch, 16th)

(Nanjing) Today's State Council meeting discussed the countermeasures to the Shanghai Ceasefire Conference, studied the six recent telegrams from Yan Huiqing, and Guo Taiqi presented the 13 negotiation sessions. As a result, the countermeasures will be determined after the results of the Geneva Special Committee's discussion are telegraphed. Regarding the issue of the Northeast refusing Gu, although the Japanese side has expressed that it does not oppose the investigation team's hope to replace Gu, this matter has no reason, because Gu's mission was given by the National Government. On this point, the central government has no room for consideration. The government will still adhere to the original policy without any change. Tells the Press He Does Not Want to Discuss the Shanghai Situation

Close Talks with Tardieu in Paris

British Prime Minister MacDonald Will Meet Him Soon

Reuters, Geneva, 16th The US Secretary of State Stimson arrived here today. According to his statement to the press, he came here as the US representative to the Disarmament Conference to seek concrete results to benefit world peace, which is the common hope. He also said that he did not want to discuss the Shanghai issue.

Reuters, Paris, 15th The US Secretary of State Stimson has arrived in Paris and immediately went to visit the French President Doumergue. Then, he had lunch with the French Prime Minister Tardieu. After the meal, the US and French Prime Ministers discussed world issues, especially focusing on disarmament. In the afternoon, Stimson received news reporters and said that the disarmament plan presented by US Representative Gibson in Geneva was not the US disarmament plan.

At 9:50, Stimson took a train to Geneva. In February, US Representative Gibson proposed in Geneva to completely abolish submarines, poison gas, and germ warfare, protect civilians from aerial bombardment, specially restrict tanks and mobile heavy artillery, and limit military spending. He also advocated extending the Washington Treaty and the London Naval Treaty.

Havas, Paris, 15th Tardieu hosted Stimson at the Foreign Ministry. After the banquet, he had another meeting with him and then received British Ambassador Lord Tyrell. At 4:30, Tardieu attended the State Council meeting and reported on the work of the Disarmament Conference. After the meeting, he received Stimson and US disarmament representative Davis and talked for an hour. Tardieu then received the press and briefly said that he was very happy to meet his old friends after 20 years. We will freely study various issues related to the two countries in a friendly spirit, and pay special attention to the issues discussed in Geneva.

Reuters, London, 15th British Prime Minister MacDonald plans to go to Geneva from London on April 20, the day after the Chancellor of the Exchequer presents the budget in the House of Commons, to personally contact French Prime Minister Tardieu, US Secretary of State Stimson, and other important politicians from various countries on international events. Important News: Five Routes of Righteous Armies Advance in Jilin 140

Wang Delin Appointed Commander-in-Chief of the National Salvation Army

Harbin-Suifenhe Line Tense, Fierce Fighting in Yanbian

Ding and Li Supplement Military Strength, Plan Counteroffensive

Harbin Dispatch: Since the 7th, the situation on the Harbin-Suifenhe line has become tense again. This is because the vanguard of the first route of the National Salvation Army, led by Liu Wankui, advanced to the Hengdaohezi station. The Zhu Lihan Regiment of the puppet Jilin army stationed at the station, equipped with machine guns and artillery, defected en masse and joined the National Salvation Army. Zhu's regiment only had three companies; two companies defected, and the remaining company was transported by freight train back to Yimianpo to join the Japanese army. On the morning of the 8th, the National Salvation Army gradually increased its forces and advanced towards the areas of Shitouhezi and Hailin station. The 26th Brigade of Xing Zhanqing, who had agreed to be incorporated by the puppet Jilin authorities, also conducted anti-Japanese activities after receiving their pay, moving diagonally to the left of the Wujimi River and threatening the rear of the Japanese army at Yimianpo. As a result, the Japanese army and the Xi Qia army were attacked from both sides. Xi's three brigades, in conjunction with the Japanese army's Amano and Hase units (one company each), are holding the Yimianpo-Zhuhe section, adopting a defensive posture and only sending aircraft for reconnaissance. The National Salvation Army is now organized into five routes, under the command of a general headquarters. The commander-in-chief is Wang Delin, and the deputy commander-in-chief is Liu Wankui. The commanders of the five routes are Wang Delin (1st route), Liu Wankui (2nd route), Jiang Haishan (3rd route), Zhang Zhibang (4th route), and Li Xiangshan (5th route). The first route also has three special operations detachments. The second and fourth routes each have a cavalry detachment. The total number of troops is over 30,000, including about 5,000 "Big Sword" and "Red Spear" troops. The general headquarters has a propaganda department, and many patriotic young volunteers are participating in the work. Each passenger and freight train from Suifenhe to Harbin has slogans such as "(Down with the puppet state of Manzhou, eliminate the traitor Xi Qia and Zhang Jinghui)" pasted on them, all of which were pasted on when the train passed Hengdaohezi. The general headquarters is currently located in Ning'an, and the deputy general headquarters is located in Maqiaohe. After Wang Delin's first route recovered Ning'an, he sent special operations detachments to actively advance towards Yanbian, intending to open up the Sino-Korean border and assist the Korean uprising. Since the 5th, the attacks on Yanji, Sandaogou, Liangshuiquanzi, and Longjingcun have been very fierce. The Chinese and Koreans oppressed by the Japanese in Yanbian have risen up in large numbers in response to the righteous cause, so Wang's first route has increased to 15,000 men. The Japanese army sent two companies of Korean troops to attack, and there were fierce battles on the 6th and 7th, with little progress. They are now planning to send another brigade to attack. The headquarters of the 2nd Division of the Japanese Kwantung Army plans to move to Wujimi in the coming days, intending to advance towards Ning'an and Muling. However, half of the three brigades under the division are scattered in various places and are being held back by the Self-Defense Army near Fangzheng, so their strength to attack Ning'an is probably not great. Fangzheng County fell on April 5th. The Japanese army entered the city at 2:00 PM on the same day. Initially, the Self-Defense Army, led by Feng Zhanhai, Zhao Yi, Gong Changhai, and Ma Xianzhang, concentrated about 10,000 men in Fangzheng and held the three key passes of Sanjiaxinzi, Gaolimaozi, and Dzigou in the south, east, and west of Fangzheng. Li Du and Ding Chao arrived at the front line on the evening of the 4th to command due to the emergency. At 5:00 AM on the 5th, the Japanese army, led by Amano and Hase and the bandit army of Yu Shencheng, totaling 8,000 men, launched a fierce attack, using tanks and armored vehicles to break through the three key passes, and six new-style aircraft of the Kwantung Army flew over the city walls and dropped bombs, totaling over a hundred. Important places in the city were destroyed, and several hundred innocent people were killed or injured. Li and Ding, believing that the city could not be defended, ordered a retreat to the Demoli, Daloulemi, and Xiaoloulebi areas north of Fangzheng at noon to establish a new defensive line. The Wakamatsu company of the Amano brigade of the Japanese army pursued greedily, and was bravely countered by the Gong Changhai brigade in Demoli. The cavalry arrived everywhere, and the enemy was forced to retreat. In this battle, over 300 Japanese soldiers were killed, and the Japanese army began to retreat in panic. The main force of the Japanese army has now been transferred back to Wujimi, leaving two companies to cooperate with the bandit army of Yu Shencheng to hold Fangzheng, and they no longer have the strength to advance further. However, Japanese aircraft, in teams of four or five, bomb Yilan all day long. At noon on the 7th, they dropped over 40 bombs, destroying over 20 civilian houses and killing over 30 soldiers and civilians. They bombed again on the 8th, destroying five market houses and killing two pedestrians. Fortunately, Li Du's arrangements were very meticulous and he had anti-aircraft guns, so he was not afraid of the harassment of Japanese aircraft. Ding and Li are also doing their best to replenish their military strength, planning a major counteroffensive in the near future. (8th)

Japanese University Professor Discusses the Pros and Cons of Leaving the League of Nations 141

Kisaburo Yokota Believes Leaving is a Mistake

Also States That Japan Cannot Act Emotionally

Dr. Yokota's Opinion: Recently, there have been many advocating withdrawal from the League of Nations, and public opinion across the country is very supportive. I believe that there is no reason whatsoever to withdraw from the League of Nations. It is meaningless from a legal standpoint and an even greater misstep from a political standpoint, being nothing more than a purely emotional reaction. From a legal standpoint, those who advocate withdrawal from the League of Nations say that severing relations with the League of Nations can avoid all kinds of interference and that the League of Nations cannot punish Japan as a defendant. This notion is completely wrong, because if Japan decides to withdraw from the League of Nations, it will take two years for it to take effect. Therefore, within two years of withdrawal, Japan must fulfill all obligations under the Covenant. If the League of Nations reviews the Manchurian incident, Japan is naturally obligated to legally comply. Even if relations with the League of Nations are severed after two years, if the Manchurian incident is not resolved after two years, Japan will still be affected by the issue and cannot escape the constraints of the League of Nations Covenant. Recently, those who advocate withdrawal often believe that joining the League of Nations is subject to various legal constraints, and that in the event of a dispute, the resolutions or recommendations of the Council and the General Assembly cannot give full play to their own will. If we withdraw now, legally, regardless of the resolutions of the Council or the recommendations of the General Assembly, without the consent of the country concerned, it will not be bound by its binding force, that is, if the whole assembly is unanimous, only Japan opposes it, it will not be bound by it. In this way, Article 15 of the Covenant can also be ignored for the Manchurian and Shanghai issues. However, the Ministry of Foreign Affairs believes that Article 11 is not important and only opposes the application of Article 15. This is not only a misinterpretation of a legitimate covenant, but in practice, there is no reason to oppose Article 15. This is because the nature of applying Article 15 is the same as applying Article 11. The difference between the two articles is only that, apart from the parties to the dispute, if a party to the dispute agrees with the unanimous recommendation of the whole assembly, the other party to the dispute must not engage in combat. However, it is clear whether Japan is engaging in combat. From a political standpoint, after Japan announces its withdrawal, it will continue to bear all the obligations of the League of Nations Covenant for two years, while losing its position as a representative of the Council and the General Assembly and abandoning various opportunities to assert its claims. As a result, the countries of the League will make judgments based solely on China's one-sided reports. Japan has lost its diplomatic position, and the intentions of various countries and world opinion are quite related. Recalling Germany before the World War, how strong its national power was and how active its military actions were during the war, why did it collapse in the end? Because the global economic blockade was the main reason. Because of the economic blockade, no matter how strong the militarism is, it cannot stand. Today, the countries of Europe, based on the experience of the past war, will use the most evil means once, what will happen? Japan already has a deep militaristic impression on the outside world, and is also actively seeking the advancement of militarism internally. Those who advocate withdrawal from the League of Nations are nothing more than the first step in implementing this policy. Their mistake is ignorance to the extreme. From this point of view, there is no reason to withdraw from the League of Nations in law or politics, there is no need to say it again.

The direct first motive of those who advocate withdrawal is the application of Article 15 of the Covenant. They believe that the League of Nations has ignored Japan's opposition and wants to apply Article 15 to the Manchurian incident. However, according to the explicit provisions of Article 15, whenever there is a dispute that threatens to sever diplomatic relations, if it is not subject to adjudication, Article 15 can automatically be applied at the request of a party to the dispute. Japan cannot blame the League of Nations for its actions. Recalling that at the beginning of the Manchurian incident, due to the conflict of forces, it was about to fall into the severance of diplomatic relations, the League of Nations automatically invoked Article 15 at China's request and naturally applied it to the Manchurian incident. Japan originally had no reason to oppose it, because when Japan joined the League of Nations, it had already agreed to the Covenant, and now it cannot contradict itself by raising objections. In short, the application of Article 15 is a fact that cannot be avoided, then those who advocate withdrawal must say that the League of Nations ignored Japan's claims and allowed China's request. Their lack of wisdom and knowledge, and their misunderstanding of the principles of the Covenant, is extreme.

The second motive of those who advocate withdrawal is that the speeches of the small countries in the League of Nations often criticize Japan from an irresponsible position. This is even more unreasonable. When Italy occupied Corfu, it was severely criticized and attacked by small countries. As a result, Italy had to yield. From this fact, it can be clearly seen that if Japan is angry at the criticism and attacks of small countries at the General Assembly, it will advocate withdrawal. Looking at the world's news magazines, the criticism and attacks of small countries are probably even worse than at the General Assembly. The League of Nations naturally uses world opinion as its guide, because the trend of world opinion can be used as a mirror of the League of Nations. By this mirror, the League of Nations can clearly observe the trend of public opinion in various countries, and Japan only uses the face of a great power as an excuse and hates the attacks of small countries. This is completely an emotional argument. Its lack of understanding is extreme. Purely emotional arguments are not conducive to Japan. However, if Japan withdraws from the League of Nations, it will inevitably be permanently condemned by the world in the future. Japan's position will not be easily reversed from now on.

The Inspection Tour of the Investigation Team From Beijing West (6) 142

Appendix: The League of Nations' Handling of the Sino-Japanese Dispute

After occupying Qiqihar, Japan concentrated its forces on the Beining Railway line in preparation for taking Jinzhou. By November 24, the Japanese vanguard had approached within 30 li east of Jinzhou. On November 25, our representative urgently appealed to the Executive Yuan, requesting the establishment of a neutral zone west and east of Jinzhou, defended by British, French, and Italian troops sent by the League of Nations. If our forces were insufficient to resist the enemy, this unavoidable measure could at least prevent the Japanese army from advancing westward. Moreover, with the defense of foreign troops, the Japanese army would certainly not dare to attack under the pretext of making trouble with foreign troops. Unfortunately, a few days later, our authorities, through the French envoy in Beiping, indicated to Japan that if the Japanese army was willing to return to Shenyang, the Chinese troops would also withdraw inside the Great Wall, which aroused the opposition of the people.

The League of Nations, while strongly in favor of the establishment of a neutral zone, was opposed by Japan to the idea of sending troops to defend it. As a result, it only allowed the British, French, and German embassies in Beiping to send personnel to consult with the commanders of the Chinese and Japanese armies on the spot to establish a neutral zone.

When the Japanese army wanted to attack Jinzhou, the reason it announced was that our troops were concentrated in the Jinzhou area, which was enough to endanger the safety of the Japanese army. In order to avoid conflict, Briand sent a telegram to the Chinese and Japanese governments on November 25, asking them to order the front-line troops to stop military vehicle movements. On November 27, the Japanese government replied to Briand, saying that if the Chinese troops could retreat into Ken City, the Japanese troops could also retreat back to Shenyang. Except when necessary to go to North China via Jinzhou to protect Japanese expatriates, the Japanese army would not cross the neutral boundary line of Jinzhou. The security from Jinzhou West to Shanhaiguan should be maintained by the local Chinese government, but the security from Jinzhou East to Shenyang should be maintained by the Shenyang government. His intention was that the security from Jinzhou to Shenyang should be managed by Japan.

On November 28, the Japanese representative sent another letter to Briand, in addition to reiterating the main points of the previous letter, and expressed dissatisfaction with the League of Nations' interference in the demarcation issue. Its intention was to point out that since our authorities had already entrusted the French minister in Beiping to directly negotiate with the Japanese government, if the League of Nations did not want to interfere, the result would delay the resolution of the issue. The next day, Briand also sent a letter in reply, but our government, due to public opposition, cancelled the previous agreement. At that time, the Japanese foreign minister resigned to the Japanese emperor because he was criticized by various countries for pressing on Jinzhou later. In order to appease the cabinet, the commander of the Kwantung Army withdrew the troops that had approached Jinzhou back to Shenyang on November 29. At this point, our representative also declared the abandonment of the principle of withdrawing troops on a regular basis. Since the meeting on November 22 adopted the principle of sending personnel to investigate, the League of Nations Secretariat and the Japanese delegation had separately engaged in drafting resolutions. Later, due to the Jinzhou neutral zone issue, the draft was shelved. After our country abandoned the request to establish a neutral zone, the Executive Yuan continued to draft the work (to be continued)

The Tragic Situation of the Spring Famine in Northern Anhui 143

Victims Compete for Fire Algae and Wheat Seedlings

Successive Deaths, Spring Epidemics Worrying

Bengbu Dispatch: Disasters in northern Anhui are frequent, the vitality of the place has been damaged, and the people's livelihoods are almost gone. The recent spring famine has led to widespread starvation. As far as the 21 counties in northern Anhui are concerned, the disaster is more serious than in central and southern Anhui, but the relief funds allocated are less, which has led to an unusually severe disaster situation in various counties recently. In counties such as Taihe, Hao County, Shou County, Fengtai, Huaiyuan, Su County, and Dingyuan, the victims, because the grain was flooded last year and there was no grain to eat, peeled off tree bark, ground it into coarse powder, mixed it with water algae, grass roots, leaves and other things, steamed it and ate it. Although it is difficult to swallow, it is better than being hungry. All rivers, streams, and swamps that produce water algae have supervisors guarding them day and night, not allowing others to steal them. Water algae on the market sells for as much as 200 coins per catty. According to Xu Baizheng, the chief of the Taihe emergency relief, the county suffered a hail disaster first, followed by flooding, and the disaster situation was the most tragic. What people would not eat in a good year and used to feed pigs, the victims are now competing to eat. Mr. Xu brought specimens of the victims' food, totaling as many as 12 kinds. After eating, the victims' faces are mostly yellow and swollen, the price of rice is like pearls and firewood like cassia, it is conceivable. Recently, tree bark and fire algae have been almost exhausted. The victims are banding together and going to the fields to cut wheat seedlings and cook them at home. However, due to the lack of nutrition, the victims' faces are swollen after eating. Therefore, personnel from Su County who came to Bengbu to receive relief advocated the distribution of edible salt to provide relief. The cooking of wheat seedlings by the victims has become a widespread phenomenon. However, in remote markets in the northwest, women and children are openly bought and sold. Such situations are often found even in Bengbu City. Moreover, the victims gather in places where they have no way to make a living and no way to beg, and they rob food everywhere. In the Suixi area of Su County, a family has been without food for several days, and the child is very hungry, crying and begging for food. The mother was pestered by the child and made a cake shape out of mud to give to the child, hoping to reduce the crying. It can also be said to be tragic. Although there are occasional porridge factories in various counties and towns, there are too many victims, and there is a feeling that there are too many monks and too little porridge, and it is impossible to benefit everyone. When the victims have been hungry for a long time, they become skinny and occasionally faint and die with clear water flowing from their mouths. The disaster area is wide, deaths are successive, and corpses are lying in the fields,无人掩埋. It is expected that when the weather is humid and warm, epidemics will inevitably occur, thinking about this, I am worried.

The Shanghai National Government Relief Water Disaster Committee released emergency relief in northern Anhui, totaling 6,730 tons of American wheat. Due to the impact of the Shanghai War, transportation was difficult, resulting in delayed inspections and releases. Later, 2,000 tons were converted into cash and released to take both into account. As for Quan Shaowu, the newly appointed director of the Anhui Northern Relief Office of the Disaster Area Working Group of the Association, who came to Bengbu, is quite lacking in handling relief matters

Representatives Guo Zhongyi and Jiang Zijing and others are particularly strong in opposition. Someone recently telegraphed Zhu Qinglan in Shanghai to ask him to punish him in order to maintain relief affairs and save the people. (April 13)

Long-Term Transactions Reach Extreme Desolation 145

The Second Extension Failed to Meet the Deadline

A General Ledger Impossible to Sort Out

Currently, six long-term settlement periods are nearing completion. The funds due in half a month must be cut off from the previous "worm me" situation. In past years, this time was so prosperous, with busy and lively transactions and considerable prices. Unexpectedly, after the Shanghai Incident, various industries stagnated. For some of the maturing funds in the financial sector, not only was it impossible to claim them back, but also the funds that should have been settled at the end of last year, which had once been transferred to the current account as long-term funds, have not been repaid a single cent to this day. Now, with the second extension of the funds due in a quarter of a month, they have failed to meet the deadline. The general ledger is simply impossible to sort out. Therefore, in the past two days, there was no clue as to how to claim the funds that were due in a quarter of a month. Naturally, it is difficult to fully supply new funds. As a result, there were only small transactions to decorate the market. It is said that yesterday's volume was only in the range of 300,000 to 400,000. Although there was no standard interest rate, it was at least above ten taels. As for long-term deposits, it is said that most are prepared to be transferred. If so, the financial sector can still cope, but there is a risk of being overwhelmed. However, the overall bleak situation is truly reminiscent of the past.

Free Talk

Bloody Record Lu 159

Long Live the Republic of China, A certain gentleman participated in the Battle of Jinan. He belonged to Su's regiment under Fang Zhenwu's command. The May 3rd Incident occurred. The isolated army defended the city. When the ammunition was exhausted, the entire nation broke through the encirclement. Crying "Long Live the Republic of China!" and holding the national emblem, his courage suddenly increased. The sound of killing shook the sky. The regiment suffered very little loss. In this Shanghai battle, the gentleman again led his troops to Shanghai to assist the 19th Route Army. In the Miaohang and Jiangwan areas, they fought fiercely for dozens of days. According to the gentleman's account, whenever in a crisis, he always used the slogan "Long Live the Republic of China!" to stir up the morale of the army, which always turned danger into safety and wiped out the captives. The speaker said, "Although we have no sharp weapons, our hot blood is indeed our sharp weapon." Therefore, the sound of "Long Live the Republic of China!" on the battlefield is the only treasure of the country and the nation.

The First Martyr of the Shanghai War. The Japanese invasion of Shanghai was sudden. It was what is called the behavior of thieves. At that time, a large contingent of our army was stationed in Zhenru. The front line of the Zhabei Railway Station was guarded by military police. At 11 p.m. on the night of January 28th, the enemy attacked with armored vehicles. The momentum was quite fierce. Our army only had short guns and stray bullets, and the disparity in numbers made it difficult to sustain. A loyal and brave nameless hero, carrying explosives, threw himself at the enemy. The bomb exploded and destroyed the vehicle. The enemy, thinking it was a landmine, was in a panic. Our army took advantage of the situation to pursue and finally won a great victory. And our Republic of China's national hero also shed blood on Baoshan Road. His loyalty and bravery will forever be known to the world. This was the first martyr of the Shanghai War.

Begonia and Butterfly Dreams in the Park 160

The scenery of Xidi Lake and Mountain is boundless. In past years, horses and carriages thronged, and men and women were like clouds. Now, all have been chased away in the chaos. Returning to the old place, I seek to relieve my boredom. I decided to enter the city park with a friend. The park used to have many flowers and trees, but they have been ravaged by wind and rain. The rouge is all in disarray. Only within a fence on the west side, several weeping begonia trees are planted. They are called "iron stems" and also "drunken beauties." The tall trunks have dense branches. The flowers bloom especially abundantly. They are round and jade-like, with powdery flesh and soft fat. The luster is like a fairy, and the charm is unmatched. It is truly like a beauty's drunken sleep. Moreover, looking around, the peach and apricot branches are almost bare, but these alone are full of smiles, just like the towering Lingguang Hall. Could it be that the weak begonia has turned into a pine and cypress that withers later? It is fitting that all the visitors in the park linger and are reluctant to leave. Thus, the beauty, with her drunkenness, turns to intoxicate the guests. Alas, what kind of world is this? Disaster is imminent. How can one get drunk in front of the flowers and end this life? Therefore, I record it with two quatrains:

The fragrant time is all entrusted to the chaos of war,

What a pity that the beautiful gardens are falling red.

Only two or three begonia trees remain,

The beauty still smiles in the spring breeze.

The landscape of broken rivers and mountains is renewed,

The spirit of flowers is seen in drunkenness.

Relying on a piece of rouge color,

Holding up the ten miles of spring in Ronghu Lake.

World News Briefs 161

If humans could travel to the moon, then a strong man weighing 175 pounds on Earth would only weigh 29 pounds on the moon.

The average lifespan of children in England in 1931 was 58 years, while the average lifespan of children born in India was only 20 to 25 years.

Due to the economic panic in England, the number of unemployed people is increasing day by day. Musical gatherings are rare, so 12,000 musicians are suffering from unemployment. In London alone, there are as many as 3,000 people.

European women's clothing is changing rapidly. The colors considered fashionable now are robin's egg blue, moonstone, valley mist, and moon shadow for evening wear, and thistle, old red, and military uniform red for daytime wear. (Seagull)

The Shanghai Battle and Armaments (11) - One Hidden 162

Tank Vehicles: Scientific advancement leads to the mechanization of military circles. The rapidity of movement, the greatness of attack power, and the possession of defensive power are improving day by day. Now, let's talk about mechanized tank vehicles. This vehicle is also known as an armored car or war chariot. There are male and female distinctions. Males are over thirty-seven tons, while females are just around twenty tons. However, they are all surrounded by steel plates. The vehicle can carry two artillery operators, two drivers, and two reconnaissance officers. It is specifically used to break through trenches and barbed wire. It can also climb mountains and cross hills. Even in dense forests, movement is very free. Therefore, it is called a land cruiser. As for the origin of the war chariot, it originated in ancient China. Sun Tzu mentioned the use of prepared war chariots. However, the war chariot at that time was a four-wheeled vehicle capable of carrying more than ten people, covered with leather to protect against arrows and stones. In the Crimean War of 1853, the British army used steam-powered vehicles to transport military supplies. Later, due to the advancement of internal combustion engines, the power of the Dissel Engine over Turfin (divided into air turbines, gas turbines, steam turbines, and hydraulic turbines) made operation convenient. Before long, a man named Thomas, Tank, Bluro from the Setford Industrial Chamber of Commerce in Setford, England, completely reformed the vehicle's structure, giving it a brand new look. Therefore, the vehicle was named after him.

[P A Heroic Death (1) - Mo Yi

"Old Zhang, it's been chaotic these past two days. We don't understand what they're doing. It wasn't until the mobilization order came down today that we knew we were going to fight the 'dwarf devils'. I heard that the 19th Route Army brothers beat the 'dwarf devils' so badly they fled in defeat. Is that really true? If it is, then I'll be happy. Ever since I was twenty years old, when my home was burned down by bandits, I've been in the army. It's been almost eight years now, and not a year has gone by that I haven't been on the front lines. Luckily, I've been lucky, and I haven't died once. But fighting, fighting, it's all been against our own people, and I'm really getting tired of it. I've always wanted to change things up, but there's never been a chance. But now it's great, we're going to fight the 'dwarf devils'. People say the 'dwarf devils' are very powerful, but I don't know if that's true. I remember that year you fought them in Jinan. What do you think of them compared to us? Damn it, powerful? I'm not afraid of the 'dwarf devils'!"

("Old Zhao, don't listen to what people say. The 'dwarf devils' only have better weapons than us, but in every other way, they can't compare to us. Remember that time in Jinan, we only had one battalion, and we repelled a regiment of them. Do you think they're any good? Didn't you fight bandits in Jiangxi last year? To be honest, the 'dwarf devils' are much easier to fight than bandits! Fighting bandits is like fighting adults, fighting 'dwarf devils' is like playing with kids. As the saying goes, 'short people have a lot of schemes,' but what's strange to me is that when it comes to fighting, why don't the 'dwarf devils' have any schemes?" Haha!") Old Zhang made a dismissive expression on his face, casually picked up a small wooden stick from the table in front of the bed, pretending to play with it, and said with a laugh ("Really? Don't fool me!: : : No matter what, whether they're powerful or weak, I'm definitely going to fight them! Old Zhang, you have to fight hard too! If you don't, humph, if anyone doesn't fight, damn it, I'll beat them to death first!") Old Zhao said excitedly, reaching out two arms from the quilt, clenching his fists, making a big circle in the air, and punching upwards, as if those two palms could kill two enemies. ("Okay, Old Zhao, it's getting late. Let's sleep. Tomorrow we have to go to the front lines to kill 'dwarf devils'!") ("Where are we going tomorrow? Zhabei? Jiangwan? Wusong? I don't want to be assigned to rear-line work.")

("Jiangwan. It's the front line. It's the very front line. Aren't you happy now?")

("Of course I'm happy. It's my bad temper, if I have something on my mind, my eyelids just won't close.: : : :") Although Old Zhao said that, his snoring was already coming from his nose.

("He said he couldn't sleep. Ha: : :") Old Zhang turned off the light and also went to sleep.

(In an instant, this room controlled by darkness was filled everywhere with the great spirit of every warrior)

On the

Cooperation between the Military and the People 163

— Rui

Soldiers protect the people with their lives, and the people pay taxes to support the soldiers. Therefore, soldiers and the people are originally on the same front line, and the relationship between them is originally very close and loving.

Now, when the country is in trouble, I think of a small piece of history from the Hongchang era. I remember the elders saying that during the Hong Yang Rebellion, those who fled to Jiangbei, upon hearing that the seven counties of Songjiang Prefecture had been recovered by Li Hongzhang's army, rushed home. At that time, the Hong Yang troops were based in the east in Suzhou and Changzhou, and in the west in Jiahe. The area around Songjiang was still disturbed and unstable, but the general population already deeply believed that Li Hongzhang could provide thorough protection, in a reliable and trustworthy manner, and everyone hurried back to their hometowns. The spirit of military-civilian cooperation at that time can be seen in general.

Now, the 19th Route Army has resisted the brutality of the Japanese for more than forty days. In the areas of Zhenru and Nanxiang, there are many stationed troops, and the sound of artillery shakes the eardrums every day. However, the general public remains calm and settled as usual. Those with money provide some money, and those with goods provide some goods. They are very polite, and they even decline with thanks. It can truly be said that they do not take a single needle or thread. This is also a manifestation of military-civilian cooperation, which is particularly rare.

Now, a month or so has passed since the ceasefire. Why is it that in the Changshu and Kunshan areas, the number of fleeing people is increasing day by day? Not only that, but even in Songjiang and Jiaxing, which are not war zones, there are countless people, young and old, fleeing to different places every day. I asked them, "The war is not tense, why are you fleeing here?" They shook their heads and refused to say. I asked, "Is your area peaceful or chaotic?" They still shook their heads and refused to say. I asked, "Since the war is not tense and the area must be peaceful, why are you fleeing to Shanghai, where rice is as precious as pearls and firewood is as expensive as gold?" They shook their heads again and refused to say. Alas! I know the reason. Is it perhaps because of the lack of cooperation between the military and the people, or perhaps too much cooperation? Originally, since there are many troops, good and bad may inevitably be mixed together, but everything depends on whether the commander is capable or not.

When the 19th Route Army was fighting bravely against the enemy, did the 19th Route Army not dig trenches? Why did the people help with smiles on their faces? Did the 19th Route Army have no supplies? Why did the people send them in thousands and tens of thousands? In short, the current army must make the people love them when they see them, and not make the people fear them when they see them. Only then can it be an army that is unique in resisting Japan, and only then can it be considered an army of our people.

Popular Literature and Art

General Ma's Song 164

— Meng Ru'an's Owner

Last autumn, General Ma's battle at Jiangqiao shook the world. I wrote a song to praise him, but when I heard of General Ma's defection, this poem was also abandoned in my worn-out box. Yesterday, I read a telegram about General Ma's reversal, which made me feel very happy. Therefore, my poem cannot but be preserved. I am recording it now to examine his future. The bandits in Guandong are all heroes, and the general's horsemanship is especially outstanding. White bones form mountains as armor rolls back, one horse is like a dragon, and ten thousand horses are choked. Suddenly, like a tiger changing, he becomes a city defender, and for ten years he sits and whistles, clearing the border dust. Not only does his mighty power shake foreign customs, but children dare not even hear his name. One morning, the drums of war sounded in Liaoyang, and the Ezo crossed the sea to plunder. The horns of Xuan Tu city sounded their death knell, and more than one hundred thousand brave soldiers were stationed in empty camps. Iron cavalry galloped across a thousand miles, and throwing their whips, they wanted to cut off the Nen River. The general clenched his fist, tore his clothes, and rose up, saying, "This is the time for a man to serve his country!" Eight thousand disciples followed like clouds, and they cheered under the tent, each ready to die. The giant blade in his hand scrapes the sky, and we will see him driving the bandits like sheep. In the ninth month, on the day of Guihai, the bandits launched a major attack, and flying ships roared, with bullets like rain. The turtle capsized the earth's hole, the river flowed backward, and blood bathed the black and yellow, making the location confusing. The general's order came out with the power of a mountain, and ten thousand horses silently emerged from the fort. The yellow clouds fell downwards, and the flags opened, and the general charged into the formation on a single horse. The red fire shattered the whale waves, and the general chased the bandits on the Jiangqiao. He turned his horse and leaped ten zhang high, and with ten charges and ten decisions, he overturned the bandit nest. It is good for a man to die on this land, and anyone who retreats will taste my bloody blade. My spirit increases, and the bandits shrink back. We continue our efforts without stopping. The sky shakes, the earth trembles, and dragons and snakes move. We only see the bandits before, and we only see the bandits behind. In the wilderness, we only hear the sound of thunder, and the heads of greedy wolves fall in pieces. The general's men and horses are all heavenly dragons. They enter the formation black and leave the formation red. The mountains and rivers north of the pass are all supported by him, and who can compare to him in first-class border merits? Alas, ever since the Hu cavalry herded the Liao wilderness, more than seventy cities have fallen at the mere sight of them. The one victory at Jiangqiao shattered the bandits' courage, and they warned each other not to offend the horses of Longjiang. Looking north across the pass, our tearful eyes are dry, and lost geese cry in the clouds. Tell the general not to change his will, and to kill the bandits with all his heart, as in the beginning. After the success, wait for a painting of Lingyan Pavilion to be made. My pen can still sing one song again and write it for you.

Spring Regret 165

— Gan Fu

I read the two poems titled "Spring Regret" in your newspaper's local supplement on the eleventh. Now I follow the original rhyme and present it to you for your consideration.

Disaster starts from internal conflicts, and I have felt pain for a long time, suffering from years of waste without caring. It is pitiful that when one insults oneself, others will also insult. A great country and rivers are regrettable and have sunk.

Fragrant sea waves overturned by butterfly matchmakers, the east wind is cunning and jealous of the flowers blooming. It is pitiful that under the spring hooves of the barbarian horses, a miserable white turns red, rolling in.

Market News 166

Seeking Poems for the "Blood Flower Collection": The Asian Culture Society, in view of the declining national power and the depressed morale of the people, feels that without promotion, there is no way to inspire them. Especially in the recent bloody battle in the Northeast and Shanghai, our country has suffered greatly from the trampling of Japanese bandits, and the tragic situation is difficult to describe in writing. Therefore, they have specially hired Mr. Li Jianweng and others to edit the "Blood Flower Collection," seeking poems that describe the displacement of the war and are full of patriotic and inspiring spirit. Whether newly written or old works, complete rhymes or long songs, all are welcome (new-style poems are also collected). Once adopted, a small remuneration will be offered. Please send your contributions to the Asian Culture Society on Kang Nao Tuo Road.

The "Plain People's Evening News" to be Published Regularly: Shanghai newspapers have always been noticed by Chinese and foreign people, but most are published in the morning. Recently, Mr. Zhang and others, due to the timeliness of news and the fluency of Huang, have specially followed the example of evening editions in major European and American ports, organized the "Plain People's Evening News," which will publish one sheet per day. Its main purpose is to explore the real needs of the people and guide the major trends of society, striving to publish true and rapid news in detail, so that people in Shanghai can learn about the current events of the day during the dimming of lights, and people in other ports can also learn about the news from the sea when the dawn breaks. The preparation of the newspaper has been completed, and it has been decided to publish it on the sixteenth of this month.

Criminal Second Instance Judgment: Appellant Mao Yusheng et al. appeals the case of embezzlement, litigation fraud, and false accusation due to dissatisfaction (Main text): The original judgment is revoked for Mao Yusheng's part. Mao Yusheng is sentenced to six months of imprisonment with a two-year suspended sentence for falsely accusing another person with the intent to subject them to criminal punishment. Mao Yusheng's appeal is rejected.

Civil Second Instance Judgment: Yi Lu Meng Shu versus Lu Weiyu for the case of unpaid debt, appeals due to dissatisfaction (Main text): The appeal is rejected. The second instance litigation costs are to be borne by the appellant.

Public Notice 1: Public Notice Regarding Auction Matters. This court is executing a case involving a debt dispute between creditor Lianhua Company and debtor Weihai Automobile Company. The following property of the debtor has been seized and appraised. The auction date is set for April 27th. The court will dispatch a clerk to direct the process server to implement the auction in coordination with court police. All citizens who wish to purchase the property should register at the process server's office of this court in order to be led to the location for viewing. Afterwards, they should follow the schedule to make a bid. If there are two or more bidders, the property will be sold to the highest bidder. The full price must be paid on the spot, and the auctioned property will be handed over for collection. All residents are hereby notified. This public notice is issued. (Details listed below): 1. Subject of the auction: One 17731, 4454 automobile. 2. Location of the property: Inside Weihaiwei Road Automobile Company. 3. Minimum price: 500 yuan. 4. Location for viewing the record: Process server's office of this court. 5. Execution clerk: Wang Zhen, Process Server: Pang Guodong. Public Notice 2: Public Notice Regarding Second Price Reduction Auction. This court is executing a case involving a debt dispute between creditor Xu Ruiqing and Li Guangyu. The following movable property of the debtor has been seized and appraised for auction. Since there were no buyers on the due date, the minimum price is reduced by one-tenth of the previous price. The auction date is set for April 21st. The court will dispatch a clerk to lead the process server and court police to the location of the movable property to implement the auction. All residents who wish to purchase the movable property should register at the process server's office of this court to be directed to the location for viewing. Afterwards, they should follow the schedule to make a bid. If there are two or more bidders, the property will be sold to the highest bidder. The full price must be paid on the spot, and the auctioned property will be handed over for collection. All residents are hereby notified. This public notice is issued. (Details listed below): 1. Subject of the auction: Movable property (separate list available). 2. Location of the property: No. 100 Broadway Road, Baifu Lane. 3. Minimum price: 183 yuan, 3 jiao, 8 fen, 4 li. 4. Location for viewing the record: Process server's office of this court. 5. Execution clerk: Wang, Process Server: Liu Yulin.

Shanghai Second Special District Local Court 168

Criminal Judgments: Police Department v. Sun Yu's Opium Case (Main Text): Sun Yu's is fined 150 yuan for possessing opium paraphernalia. If unable to pay, one day of imprisonment will be substituted for every two yuan. The number of days of detention before the judgment is finalized will be offset against the fine at a rate of two yuan per day. One opium pipe, one opium lamp, and one opium needle are all confiscated and burned.

▲ Police Department v. Lin Song's Opium Case (Main Text): Lin Song is fined 60 yuan for possessing opium paraphernalia. If unable to pay, one day of imprisonment will be substituted for every two yuan. The number of days of detention before the judgment is finalized will be offset against the fine at a rate of two yuan per day. One opium pipe, one opium lamp, one opium needle, one opium tongs, and one opium tray are all confiscated and burned.

▲ Police Department v. Wu Xinji's Opium Case (Main Text): Wu Xinji is sentenced to one month of imprisonment for smoking opium. The number of days of detention before the judgment is finalized will be offset against the imprisonment at a rate of one day for every two days. One opium pipe, one opium lamp, one opium scraper, one opium tongs, one opium tray, and five opium dross balls are all confiscated and burned.

▲ Police Department v. Han Mengsheng's Opium Case (Main Text): Han Mengsheng is fined 80 yuan for possessing opium paraphernalia. If unable to pay, one day of imprisonment will be substituted for every two yuan. The number of days of detention before the judgment is finalized will be offset against the fine at a rate of two yuan per day. One opium pipe, one opium lamp, and one opium needle are all confiscated and burned.

▲ Police Department v. Viknarski et al. Assault Case (Main Text): This public prosecution is not accepted.

▲ Police Department v. Olipyng et al. Assault Case (Main Text): This public prosecution is not accepted.

▲ Police Department v. Zhang Axin's Theft Case (Main Text): Zhang Axin is sentenced to 30 days of detention for the crime of theft. The number of days of detention before the judgment is finalized will be offset against the detention at a rate of one day for every two days.

▲ Police Department v. Lu Baosheng's Opium Case (Main Text): Lu Baosheng is fined 80 yuan for possessing opium paraphernalia with intent to use it for criminal purposes. If unable to pay, one day of imprisonment will be substituted for every two yuan. The number of days of detention before the judgment is finalized will be offset against the fine at a rate of two yuan per day. One opium pipe, one opium lamp, one opium needle, and one opium tray are all confiscated and burned.

▲ Police Department v. Di Laogen's Gambling Case (Main Text): Di Laogen is fined 100 yuan for the crime of jointly gambling for money. If the fine is not paid, imprisonment will be substituted at a rate of one day for every two yuan. The number of days of detention before the judgment is finalized will be offset against the fine at a rate of 1.1 yuan per day. Gambling funds and gambling paraphernalia are confiscated according to the list.

▲ Police Department v. Wei A'ming et al. Opium Case (Main Text): Wei A'ming is sentenced to six months of imprisonment and fined 150 yuan for the crime of helping with the intention of profit by providing a place for people to smoke opium substitutes. Xu De and Liu Fengchun are each sentenced to two months of imprisonment and fined 40 yuan for the crime of smoking opium substitutes. If the fines are converted to imprisonment, one day of imprisonment will be substituted for every two yuan. The number of days of detention before the judgment is finalized will be offset against the imprisonment at a rate of one day for every two days. Red pills, opium pipes, opium lamps, etc., are confiscated according to the list.

Civil Judgments: Fang Xingbang and Xing Bingqing et al.'s Objection to Execution Case (Main Text): The plaintiff's claim is rejected; the litigation costs are to be borne by the plaintiff.

▲ Hengji Account Room Xiao Yuanpiao v. Huang Wanqing's Debt Case (Main Text): The plaintiff's claim is rejected; the litigation costs are to be borne by the plaintiff.

▲ Osland v. Koshnitzky's Debt Case (Main Text): The defendants shall be jointly and severally liable to repay the plaintiff 1,206 taels and 2 mace of silver, as well as interest at an annual rate of 5% from the date of filing the lawsuit until the date of completion of execution, and compensate the plaintiff's attorney's fees of 50 taels of silver. The remainder of the plaintiff's claim is rejected; the litigation costs are to be borne jointly and severally by the defendants. The first item of this judgment shall be subject to provisional execution.

▲ Jiuhua Food Company v. Du Bolunji's Goods Debt Case (Main Text): The defendant shall pay the plaintiff's goods debt of 1,065 yuan and 2 jiao and 9 fen. The litigation costs shall be borne by the defendant.

▲ Tang Daohong v. Chen Dayou's Debt Case (Main Text): The defendant shall pay the plaintiff 120 yuan. The litigation costs shall be borne by the defendant.

▲ Sen Kemang v. Li Wen's Debt Case (Main Text): The defendant shall repay the plaintiff 328 yen and 9 jiao and 5 fen, as well as interest at an annual rate of 5% from the date of filing the lawsuit until the date of completion of execution. The plaintiff's request for provisional execution is rejected; the litigation costs shall be borne by the defendant.

▲ Du Zimei v. Chen Xingxun's Rent Arrears Case (Main Text): The defendant shall pay the plaintiff 400 yuan in rent; the litigation costs shall be borne by the defendant.

▲ Pan Zhaobang v. Hu Kailin's Rent Arrears Case (Main Text): The defendant shall pay the plaintiff 105 yuan in rent; the litigation costs shall be borne by the defendant.

▲ Ha Jalassen v. Che Nahuieski et al.'s Loan Case (Main Text): The defendant Che Nahuieski shall repay the plaintiff 200 yuan, as well as interest at an annual rate of 5% from the date of the loan until the date of completion of execution. If the execution is ineffective, Darleski shall pay on his behalf. The litigation costs shall be borne equally by the defendants.

▲ China Paint Material Company v. Sen Dalin Trademark Goods Debt Case (Main Text): The defendant shall repay the plaintiff 560 yuan, 0 jiao and 9 cents. The litigation costs shall be borne by the defendant.

▲ Yao Wende Hall v. Qiu Zhongyuan's Rent and Return of Property Case (Main Text): The defendant shall pay the plaintiff 260 yuan in rent. The remainder of the plaintiff's claim is rejected; the plaintiff shall bear one-fifth of the litigation costs, and the defendant shall bear four-fifths.

▲ Wu Tiansheng v. Yuanlai Barber Shop Owner Zheng Rongqing's Rice Debt Case (Main Text): The defendant shall pay the rice debt of 7 yuan and 9 jiao. The litigation costs shall be borne by the defendant. This judgment is subject to provisional execution.

▲ Chu Xiaoqing v. Gu Ande's Advance Payment Case (Main Text): The plaintiff's claim is rejected; the litigation costs shall be borne by the plaintiff. (Above, April 16th)
